Time stamp string length. The string format is \char`\"{}yy/\+M\+M/dd,hh\+:mm\+:ss+/-\/zz\char`\"{} (Year/\+Month/\+Day,Hour\+:\+Min\+:Seconds+/-\/\+Time\+Zone). One extra byte is added for the null character. \index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}!L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+S\+\_\+\+U\+C\+S2\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES@{L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+S\+\_\+\+U\+C\+S2\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES}}
\index{L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+S\+\_\+\+U\+C\+S2\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES@{L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+S\+\_\+\+U\+C\+S2\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+B\+Y\+T\+ES}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}}

Connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Block until the service is available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Create@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Create}}

\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__sms__interface_8h_aca1691010c88995cb47225f2889910fa}{}\label{le__sms__interface_8h_aca1691010c88995cb47225f2889910fa}
Delete a Message data structure.

It deletes the Message data structure and all the allocated memory is freed. If several users own the Message object (e.\+g., several handler functions registered for S\+MS message reception), the Message object will only be deleted if one User owns the Message object.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em msg\+Ref} & Reference to the message object. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Disconnect the current client thread from the service providing this A\+PI.

Normally, this function doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called. After this function is called, there\textquotesingle{}s no longer a connection to the service, and the functions in this A\+PI can\textquotesingle{}t be used. Get the binary Message.

Output parameters are updated with the binary message content and the length of the raw binary message in bytes. If the binary data exceed the value of \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} input parameter, a L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW error code is returned and \textquotesingle{}raw\textquotesingle{} is filled until \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} bytes.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR Message is not in binary format 

L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW Message length exceed the maximum length. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Output parameters are updated with the P\+DU message content and the length of the P\+DU message in bytes. If the P\+DU data exceed the value of \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} input parameter, a L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW error code is returned and \textquotesingle{}pdu\textquotesingle{} is filled until \textquotesingle{}len\textquotesingle{} bytes.

L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.

Get the U\+C\+S2 Message (16-\/bit format).

Output parameters are updated with the U\+C\+S2 message content and the number of characters. If the U\+C\+S2 data exceed the value of the length input parameter, a L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW error code is returned and \textquotesingle{}ucs2\+Ptr\textquotesingle{} is filled until of the number of chars specified.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+M\+A\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR Message is not in binary format
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW Message length exceed the maximum length.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em msg\+Ref} & Reference to the message object. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ucs2\+Ptr} & U\+C\+S2 message. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in,out}  & {\em ucs2\+Size\+Ptr} & \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Set the Telephone destination number.

Telephone number is defined in I\+T\+U-\/T recommendations E.\+164/E.163. E.\+164 numbers can have a maximum of fifteen digits and are usually written with a \textquotesingle{}+\textquotesingle{} prefix.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED Message is Read-\/\+Only. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER Telephone destination number length is equal to zero. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If telephone destination number is too long is too long (max L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+D\+M\+D\+E\+F\+S\+\_\+\+P\+H\+O\+N\+E\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return.

If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Set the S\+MS center address.

S\+MS center address number is defined in I\+T\+U-\/T recommendations E.\+164/E.163. E.\+164 numbers can have a maximum of fifteen digits and are usually written with a \textquotesingle{}+\textquotesingle{} prefix.

This function must be called to set the Text Message content.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED Message is Read-\/\+Only. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER Text message length is equal to zero. 

L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Text Message is encoded in A\+S\+C\+II format (I\+S\+O8859-\/15) and characters have to exist in the G\+SM 23.\+038 7 bit alphabet.

If message is too long (max L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+S\+\_\+\+T\+E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), it is a fatal error, the function will not return.

If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it is a fatal error, the function will not return. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Stop to count the messages successfully received and sent. \index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_sms_TryConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+sms\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__sms__interface_8h_a59dc61c13191d632d08c576ee165c5bc}{}\label{le__sms__interface_8h_a59dc61c13191d632d08c576ee165c5bc}
Try to connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Return with an error if the service is not available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK if the client connected successfully to the service.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if the server is not currently offering the service to which the client is bound.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED if the client interface is not bound to any service (doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a binding).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the Service Directory cannot be reached. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
